{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01NDo59SuPZvVQLLsjSMoSmp","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_011ftSzMFMqiMWBcbZaqSxFM","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nThese release notes document the API and configuration changes in Flipt since v1.40.1, including new features, improvements, and important information for upgrading.\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nNo breaking changes identified in this release. All API changes are backward compatible.\n\n## New Features\n\n### Configuration: Remote Blob Storage Support\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nFlipt now supports loading configuration files from remote blob storage backends. This enables storing your Flipt configuration in cloud object storage (S3, Azure Blob Storage, Google Cloud Storage) instead of local filesystem.\n\n#### Supported Schemes\n- **S3:** `s3://bucket-name/path/to/config.yml`\n- **Azure Blob Storage:** `azblob://container/path/to/config.yml`\n- **Google Cloud Storage:** `gs://bucket-name/path/to/config.yml`\n\n#### Configuration Example\n```bash\n# Load configuration from S3\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=s3://my-bucket/flipt-config.yml\n\n# Load configuration from Azure Blob Storage\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=azblob://mycontainer/flipt-config.yml\n\n# Load configuration from Google Cloud Storage\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=gs://my-bucket/flipt-config.yml\n```\n\n#### API Details\n- Configuration is loaded via the `getConfigFile()` function in `internal/config/config.go`\n- The function supports URLs with schemes mapped to object storage backends\n- Falls back to local filesystem if no recognized remote scheme is detected\n- Requires appropriate cloud provider credentials/authentication configured in your environment\n\n#### Migration Path\nNo migration needed. This is a new optional feature. You can continue using local configuration paths or migrate by:\n1. Upload your current `flipt.yml` to your cloud storage\n2. Set `FLIPT_CONFIG_PATH` environment variable to the remote URL\n3. Restart Flipt\n\n---\n\n### Tracing: Sampling Ratio Configuration\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nEnhanced OpenTelemetry tracing instrumentation with configurable trace sampling ratio. This allows you to control the percentage of requests that generate traces, reducing overhead in high-traffic environments.\n\n#### Configuration Schema\n\n**YAML Configuration:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:4317\n```\n\n**Environment Variable:**\n```bash\nFLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.1\n```\n\n#### Valid Values\n- Minimum: `0` (no traces sampled)\n- Maximum: `1` (all traces sampled, default)\n- Recommended for production: `0.1` to `0.5`\n\n#### Configuration Details\n- **Type:** Float64 (0.0 - 1.0)\n- **Default:** `1` (sample all traces)\n- **Validation:** Flipt validates that the value is between 0 and 1 at startup\n\n#### Implementation\n- Implemented using OpenTelemetry SDK's `TraceIDRatioBased` sampler\n- Applied at the TracerProvider level in `internal/tracing/tracing.go`\n- Sampler is initialized with: `tracesdk.TraceIDRatioBased(cfg.SamplingRatio)`\n\n#### API Example\nWhen creating a tracer provider programmatically:\n```go\ncfg := config.TracingConfig{\n    Enabled: true,\n    Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,\n    SamplingRatio: 0.1,\n}\nprovider, err := tracing.NewProvider(ctx, version, cfg)\n```\n\n#### Migration Path\n- This is a new optional feature; no migration required\n- Default behavior (sample all traces) unchanged unless explicitly configured\n- To reduce sampling:\n  1. Update your configuration file or environment variable\n  2. Set `samplingRatio` to desired value (e.g., `0.1` for 10%)\n  3. Restart Flipt\n\n---\n\n### Analytics: Entity ID Tracking\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nEntity ID is now tracked in analytics data when using ClickHouse as the analytics backend. This enables better insights into which entities are being evaluated.\n\n#### Details\n- Entity ID values are now captured and stored in the analytics event stream\n- Tracked in addition to existing metrics (flag key, namespace, etc.)\n- Applies to ClickHouse analytics backend\n- Analytics can be queried to analyze entity usage patterns\n\n#### Configuration\nNo new configuration required. If you have ClickHouse analytics enabled, entity ID tracking is automatic:\n\n```yaml\nanalytics:\n  storage:\n    type: clickhouse\n    clickhouse:\n      endpoint: http://localhost:8123\n```\n\n---\n\n## Improvements\n\n### Authentication: Database Connection Optimization\n\n**Fixed in:** v1.40.1 (includes auth improvements)\n\nAuthentication backend now avoids establishing unnecessary database connections:\n- Connections are only established when authentication methods require them\n- Reduces database connection pool overhead\n- Improves startup time for authentication configurations that don't need a database\n\n#### Details\n- Applied in `internal/server/authn/` module\n- Only methods like token authentication that require database access will establish connections\n- Methods like OAuth/OIDC that don't need database remain lightweight\n\n---\n\n### Authentication: Cache Optimization\n\n**Fixed in:** v1.40.1\n\nAuthentication hash caching now stores only the hash rather than full authentication data:\n- Reduces cache memory usage\n- Improves cache performance\n- More secure (hashes instead of full auth data in cache)\n\n#### Implementation\n- Cache middleware in `internal/server/middleware/`\n- Only authentication hash is cached (`auth.Hash`)\n- Full authentication data still retrieved as needed\n\n---\n\n### OpenTelemetry Resource Attributes\n\n**Improved in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nOpenTelemetry tracing now includes enhanced resource information:\n- Service name: `flipt`\n- Service version: Current Flipt version\n- OTEL environment variables: Automatically detected from environment\n- Telemetry SDK information: Included in traces\n- Container information: Detected if running in container\n- Host information: System hostname/IP included\n- Process runtime details: Go version and runtime information\n\n#### Details\n- Implements OpenTelemetry semantic conventions v1.24.0\n- Applied when creating trace resource in `internal/tracing/tracing.go`\n- Configured in `newResource()` function with:\n  - `resource.WithFromEnv()` - picks up OTEL_* environment variables\n  - `resource.WithTelemetrySDK()` - includes SDK version\n  - `resource.WithContainer()` - container detection\n  - `resource.WithHost()` - hostname/IP\n  - `resource.WithProcessRuntime*()` - runtime details\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n> **Deprecated since:** v1.36.0\n> **Will be removed:** ~1 year from deprecation date\n\nThe Jaeger tracing exporter is deprecated. OpenTelemetry dropped support for direct Jaeger export in July 2023. Jaeger officially recommends using OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol).\n\n#### Migration Path\n\n**Before:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger\n  jaeger:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n**After (using OTLP with Jaeger receiver):**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:4317  # Jaeger OTLP gRPC receiver\n```\n\nFor Jaeger containers, use OpenTelemetry Collector or update your Jaeger deployment to use OTLP receivers.\n\n---\n\n### List Pagination: Offset Parameter\n\n> **Deprecated since:** v1.13.0\n> **Status:** Active (will be removed in a future release)\n\nThe `offset` parameter in list API calls is deprecated in favor of `page_token` for forward-compatible pagination.\n\n#### Affected API Methods\n- `ListFlagRequest`\n- `ListSegmentRequest`\n- `ListRuleRequest`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest`\n\n#### Migration Path\n\n**Before:**\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\n```\n\n**After:**\n```bash\n# First request\ncurl http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10\n\n# Response includes:\n# {\n#   \"flags\": [...],\n#   \"next_page_token\": \"eyJvZmZzZXQiOjEwfQ==\"\n# }\n\n# Next page request\ncurl http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=eyJvZmZzZXQiOjEwfQ==\n```\n\n#### REST API Mapping (gRPC Gateway)\n```proto\n// Old way (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 offset = 2 [deprecated = true];  // ← Deprecated\n}\n\n// New way\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  string page_token = 3;  // ← Use this instead\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## API Updates\n\n### EvaluationResponse Changes\n\nThe `EvaluationResponse` protobuf message includes the following structure:\n\n```proto\nmessage EvaluationResponse {\n  string request_id = 1;\n  string entity_id = 2;\n  map<string, string> request_context = 3;\n  bool match = 4;\n  string flag_key = 5;\n  string segment_key = 6 [deprecated = true];      // ← Use segment_keys instead\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 7;\n  string value = 8;\n  double request_duration_millis = 9;\n  string attachment = 10;\n  EvaluationReason reason = 11;\n  string namespace_key = 12;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 13;               // ← Multiple segments supported\n}\n```\n\n**Important:**\n- `segment_key` (singular) is deprecated. Use `segment_keys` (plural) which supports multiple segments\n- All segment keys are returned in the repeated `segment_keys` field\n\n### Flag Type Support\n\nThe API supports two flag types via the `FlagType` enum:\n\n```proto\nenum FlagType {\n  VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE = 0;   // Original flag type with variants\n  BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE = 1;   // Boolean true/false flags\n}\n```\n\nBoth types are fully supported in:\n- Flag evaluation (`Evaluate` and `BatchEvaluate`)\n- Flag management (CRUD operations)\n- Rules and rollouts\n- Segments and constraints\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Prerequisites\n- Current Flipt version: v1.40.1 or later\n- Backup your database (recommended)\n- Note your current configuration for reference\n\n### Step 1: Update Flipt Binary\n\nDownload and install the latest Flipt release:\n\n```bash\n# macOS (Homebrew)\nbrew upgrade flipt\n\n# Linux (manual download)\nwget https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/releases/download/vX.Y.Z/flipt_linux_amd64.tar.gz\ntar -xzf flipt_linux_amd64.tar.gz\nsudo mv flipt /usr/local/bin/\n```\n\n### Step 2: Review Configuration Changes (Optional)\n\nIf using tracing, you may want to add sampling configuration to reduce trace volume:\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n```\n\n### Step 3: (Optional) Enable Remote Configuration\n\nIf you want to store configuration in cloud storage:\n\n1. Ensure service has appropriate cloud credentials\n\n### Step 4: Restart Flipt\n\n```bash\n# Stop the current instance\nsudo systemctl stop flipt\n\n# Start the new version\nsudo systemctl start flipt\n\n# Verify it's running\ncurl http://localhost:8080/health\n```\n\n### Step 5: Verify Functionality\n\nTest core features:\n\n```bash\n# Check server info\ncurl http://localhost:8080/api/v1/meta/info\n\n# List flags (using new pagination if needed)\ncurl http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10\n\n# Test evaluation\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8080/api/v1/evaluate \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -d '{\n    \"flagKey\": \"my-flag\",\n    \"entityId\": \"user-123\"\n  }'\n```\n\n### Step 6: Monitor for Issues\n\nWatch logs and metrics for any issues:\n\n```bash\n# Check Flipt logs (adjust path based on your setup)\njournalctl -u flipt -f\n\n# Monitor metrics if using Prometheus\n# Check http://localhost:8080/metrics\n```\n\n### Rollback Plan\n\nIf you encounter issues:\n\n1. Stop the new Flipt version\n2. Restore the previous binary version\n3. Restart Flipt with the previous version\n4. Database is compatible, no migration needed\n\n---\n\n## Storage Backend Support\n\n### Database\n- SQLite (default)\n- PostgreSQL\n- MySQL\n- CockroachDB\n- LibSQL / Turso\n\n### Filesystem/Git\n- Local directory\n- Git repository (with polling)\n- S3\n- Azure Blob Storage\n- Google Cloud Storage\n- OCI (via registries)\n\n### Caching\n- In-memory (default)\n- Redis\n\n### Analytics\n- ClickHouse (with new entity ID tracking)\n\n---\n\n## Performance Recommendations\n\n1. **For Tracing:** Set `samplingRatio` to `0.1` or lower in production to reduce overhead\n2. **For Authentication:** Let Flipt optimize connections automatically; no configuration needed\n3. **For Remote Configuration:** Use regional cloud storage to reduce latency\n\n---\n\n## Support & Documentation\n\n- **Documentation:** https://flipt.io/docs\n- **GitHub Issues:** https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues\n- **Discussions:** https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/discussions\n\n---\n\n## Version Information\n\n- **Latest Release:** v1.40.1 (2024-04-11)\n- **Current Development:** After v1.40.1\n- **API Version:** v1 (REST), Protobuf (gRPC)\n- **Minimum Go Version:** 1.20+\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5969,"cache_read_input_tokens":84343,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":5969},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"30a52af0-498b-4d53-80e9-38dc40dea12c","uuid":"bb5318cf-367a-474b-a695-31c6829121b1"}

All API changes are backward compatible.\n\n## New Features\n\n### Configuration: Remote Blob Storage Support\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nFlipt now supports loading configuration files from remote blob storage backends. This enables storing your Flipt configuration in cloud object storage (S3, Azure Blob Storage, Google Cloud Storage) instead of local filesystem.\n\n#### Supported Schemes\n- **S3:** `s3://bucket-name/path/to/config.yml`\n- **Azure Blob Storage:** `azblob://container/path/to/config.yml`\n- **Google Cloud Storage:** `gs://bucket-name/path/to/config.yml`\n\n#### Configuration Example\n```bash\n# Load configuration from S3\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=s3://my-bucket/flipt-config.yml\n\n# Load configuration from Azure Blob Storage\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=azblob://mycontainer/flipt-config.yml\n\n# Load configuration from Google Cloud Storage\nFLIPT_CONFIG_PATH=gs://my-bucket/flipt-config.yml\n```\n\n#### API Details\n- Configuration is loaded via the `getConfigFile()` function in `internal/config/config.go`\n- The function supports URLs with schemes mapped to object storage backends\n- Falls back to local filesystem if no recognized remote scheme is detected\n- Requires appropriate cloud provider credentials/authentication configured in your environment\n\n#### Migration Path\nNo migration needed. This is a new optional feature. You can continue using local configuration paths or migrate by:\n1. Upload your current `flipt.yml` to your cloud storage\n2. Set `FLIPT_CONFIG_PATH` environment variable to the remote URL\n3. Restart Flipt\n\n---\n\n### Tracing: Sampling Ratio Configuration\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nEnhanced OpenTelemetry tracing instrumentation with configurable trace sampling ratio. This allows you to control the percentage of requests that generate traces, reducing overhead in high-traffic environments.\n\n#### Configuration Schema\n\n**YAML Configuration:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:4317\n```\n\n**Environment Variable:**\n```bash\nFLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.1\n```\n\n#### Valid Values\n- Minimum: `0` (no traces sampled)\n- Maximum: `1` (all traces sampled, default)\n- Recommended for production: `0.1` to `0.5`\n\n#### Configuration Details\n- **Type:** Float64 (0.0 - 1.0)\n- **Default:** `1` (sample all traces)\n- **Validation:** Flipt validates that the value is between 0 and 1 at startup\n\n#### Implementation\n- Implemented using OpenTelemetry SDK's `TraceIDRatioBased` sampler\n- Applied at the TracerProvider level in `internal/tracing/tracing.go`\n- Sampler is initialized with: `tracesdk.TraceIDRatioBased(cfg.SamplingRatio)`\n\n#### API Example\nWhen creating a tracer provider programmatically:\n```go\ncfg := config.TracingConfig{\n    Enabled: true,\n    Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,\n    SamplingRatio: 0.1,\n}\nprovider, err := tracing.NewProvider(ctx, version, cfg)\n```\n\n#### Migration Path\n- This is a new optional feature; no migration required\n- Default behavior (sample all traces) unchanged unless explicitly configured\n- To reduce sampling:\n  1. Update your configuration file or environment variable\n  2. Set `samplingRatio` to desired value (e.g., `0.1` for 10%)\n  3. Restart Flipt\n\n---\n\n### Analytics: Entity ID Tracking\n\n**Added in:** Unreleased (after v1.40.1)\n\nEntity ID is now tracked in analytics data when using ClickHouse as the analytics backend. This enables better insights into which entities are being evaluated.\n\n#### Details\n- Entity ID values are now captured and stored in the analytics event stream\n- Tracked in addition to existing metrics (flag key, namespace, etc.)\n- Applies to ClickHouse analytics backend\n- Analytics can be queried to analyze entity usage patterns\n\n#### Configuration\nNo new configuration required. If you have ClickHouse analytics enabled, entity ID tracking is automatic:\n\n```yaml\nanalytics:\n  storage:\n    type: clickhouse\n    clickhouse:\n      endpoint: http://localhost:8123\n```\n\n---\n\n## Improvements\n\n### Authentication: Database Connection Optimization\n\n**Fixed in:** v1.40.1 (includes auth improvements)\n\nAuthentication backend now avoids
